<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникум</a> (10198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Technikum</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">technikum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникум</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">téxnikum</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникума</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникумы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникумов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>technical college, technical school, vocational school, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/technicum" class="extiw" title="w:technicum">technicum</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">institution of [further education] at an intermediate level</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***течь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>течь</a> (25749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>те́чи</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">teči</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*teťi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tekʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run, flow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>те́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">téčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вытечь.html>вы́течь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стечь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flow, to run, to stream, to move</li>
<li>to leak</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекать.html>стека́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">втека́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vtekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вытекать.html>вытека́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vytekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>течь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>те́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>те́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>те́чей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>leak
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:течь.html>течь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ <b>tečʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spring a <b>leak</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тешить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тешить.html>тешить</a> (19334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тѣшити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">těšiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*těšiti</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тихий.html>ти́хий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tíxij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quiet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тешить.html>те́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">téšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поте́шить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to amuse, to entertain
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Ф. Д. <a href = vnd.unilang:крюк.html>Крюко́в</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:обвал.html>Обва́л</a></i> 1917:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ясно.html>я́сно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проигранный.html>прои́грано</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a> подавляется <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тешить.html>те́шат</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легенда.html>леге́ндами</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jásno odnó, što délo proígrano, dvižénije podavljajetsja i ljúdi <b>téšat</b> sebjá legéndami</i></dd><dd>one thing is clear: the case is lost, the movement is suppressed and people <b>amuse</b> themselves with legends</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to comfort, to console</li>
<li>to please</li></ol>

***тешиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тешиться.html>тешиться</a> (31754)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тешить.html>те́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">téšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тешиться.html>те́шиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">téšitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поте́шиться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to amuse oneself, to have fun</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to jeer, to mock</li></ol>

***тикать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тикать.html>тика́ть</a> (12174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic. From the tick-tack sound of a clock.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тикать.html>ти́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tíkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ти́кнуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to <a href = vnd.unilang:тик.html>tick</a> (of a clock)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">тіка́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tikáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́на</a> (10202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tīmnā</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tīnā</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тина.html>ти́н</a></b>)

***тип.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> (794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τύπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">túpos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mark, impression, type</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare also the colloquial meaning of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">τύπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">týpos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">man, guy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tip</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>type, model</li>
<li>character</li>
<li class="senseid" id="Russian-Q5"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sometimes derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> man, guy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> phylum</li></ol>

***типично.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чно</a> (13676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tipíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tipíčno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-типи́чно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)типи́чнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-типи́чно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)типи́чней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>typically</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tipíčno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>it is typical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подобный.html>подо́бные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>ве́щи</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja nejó <b>tipíčno</b> govorítʹ podóbnyje véšči</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>it is typical</b> of her to say such things</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чно</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́ли</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>tipíčno</b>, što vy ob étom zabýli!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">how <b>typical</b> of you to have forgotten about it!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:типичный.html>типи́чно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tipíčno</span>)
</p>

***типовой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:типовой.html>типово́й</a> (20509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tip</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:типовой.html>типово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tipovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> type
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:типовой.html>типово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tipovój</b> vid</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>type</b> species</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> standard, model
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:типовой.html>типова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:модель.html>моде́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tipovája</b> modɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standard model</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тире.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тир.html>тире</a> (22496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tiret</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тир.html>тире́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tirɛ́</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dash</li>
<li>dash, dah <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in Morse code</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1972</b>,  Давид Тухманов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Tukhmanov" class="extiw" title="w:David Tukhmanov">David Tukhmanov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>Мой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:адрес.html>а́дрес</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:советский.html>Советский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>Сою́з</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a>, то́чки-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:тир.html>тире́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:телеграфный.html>телегра́фные</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:искать.html>ищи́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йках</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy, tóčki-<b>tirɛ́</b> telegráfnyje, iščíte na strójkax menjá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">(You) telegraphic dots and <b>dashes</b>, look for me on construction sites.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***тискать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тискать.html>ти́скать</a> (17436)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тискати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tiskati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tìskati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тискать.html>ти́скать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tískatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тиснуть.html>ти́снуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squeeze, to press</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to snuggle, to hug (pets, little kids)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to print, to publish</li></ol>
